Environment: The environment of the newly opened hotel is undisputed and very good
Facilities: The hotel swimming pool ğŸˆšï¸, but it is understandable to adapt to the room rate, and the maintenance cost needs to be considered
Service: The enthusiasm of the service staff in all positions is commendable. Everyone regards their work as a very important part and is very dedicated, but the professionalism is questionable. First, the front desk cannot properly handle each group of guests when encountering peak passenger flow. Second, the attitude of the front desk of the breakfast restaurant towards the guests staying in the hotel is stiff. As a customer, you can understand that the hotel does not allow guests staying in the hotel to enter the restaurant wearing the hotel's spare slippers, but I hope that the hotel can declare it in advance when checking in or in a conspicuous place on the packaging of the spare slippers, instead of directly intercepting customers at the entrance of the restaurant. Please also train the staff on service language
Breakfast: The variety is very rich and the taste is good, but the food is not replenished in time, and there are not enough cooking staff in the open area.

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Cozy 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:7 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted February 5, 2024
msg:The second stop of this trip to Shandong was Tai'an. I chose this hotel among many star-rated hotels. The hotel is very new and has good facilities. The shower water heats up quickly and is large. The room is large compared to other hotels of the same star rating.
The reception staff was warm, thoughtful and generous. When they knew that I came to Tai'an to climb Mount Tai, but had to leave early due to heavy snow, they specially gave me a stone talisman. Although the gift was small, it touched my heart and made up for my regret.
The hotel has a good location. Wanda is across the road. It takes more than 10 yuan to take a taxi to the high-speed rail station. It is also close to Hongmen and takes less than 20 yuan to take a taxi. Tai'an Old Street is not far away. It is recommended that friends who come to Tai'an for tourism and business trips can choose this hotel.
If I have the opportunity to come to Tai'an again, I will choose this hotel again. After all, Mount Tai has not been climbed yet.

msg:I came to Tai'an on a business trip and chose this hotel after reading reviews on Ctrip. Before I came, I called the front desk to inquire about the location. The guy at the front desk very gently introduced the location and surrounding conditions in detail. It takes 10 minutes to take a taxi from Tai'an Station to the hotel. Opposite the hotel is Wanda Plaza, which is very convenient for eating and traveling. Xiao Qi and Xiao Li at the front desk, as well as the front desk manager, were very enthusiastic and responsible. During my stay, I asked many questions and patiently answered them. The hotel is newly opened, the hygiene is first-class, the breakfast is rich, and the hotel room also has many thoughtful little details, such as a helipad on the desk and washbasin, which is convenient for placing mobile phones. There is a separate business area with computers and printers, which is the first choice for business travelers. All in all, the stay experience was great, five-star rating.
